5896h, 5943m, 6240e, 10p, 26140en, 27216w exkb-
POLITICS NEWS #1544
Date: 10/23/2009 at 1:27
From:
To  : Everyone
Subj: Hemp Wars

The Hemp Wars between the villages of Delport and Stewartsville break out as the human villagers 
engage in a fierce economic struggle. No longer caring about the politics of the Basin, the Village 
of Delport declares itself free and no longer under the sphere of influence of the Great Alliance of
Glomdoring, and the Village of Stewartsville declares itself free and no longer under the sphere of 
influence of the Great Alliance of Glomdoring.

The Village of Delport has called down a temporary spell of peace to protect its borders, declaring 
that it does not ever wish war within its borders at any time.

5896h, 5586m, 5601e, 6p, 26108en, 26943w exkb-
The Portals of Glomdoring. (Glomdoring Forest.)
The shadowy outline of a twisted forest casts a dark gloom here. The cylindrical chamber has been 
carved from marble veined with dark sediment, and polished to a lustrous smooth shine. Concentric 
circles are inlaid upon the floor, alternating with rings of black opal, onyx and dark amethyst. 
High above, the ceiling shines with a bright light that pulsates softly and steadily like a 
heartbeat. The air itself is charged with energy, veritably crackling with power. A young female 
horse with a snow white tail stands here, pawing the ground. Krellan Ysav'rai, Talons of Crow is 
here, shrouded. He wields an athame dagger in his left hand and a mystic cudgel in his right. You 
see a sign here instructing you to use the PORTAL command to enter the aetherplex system. There is 
an aetherways portal here.
You see a single exit leading out.

5896h, 5943m, 6240e, 10p, 26140en, 27181w exkb-
Great Southern Highway by Stewartsville. (road). (lost) (Great Southern Highway.)
The shadowy outline of a twisted forest casts a dark gloom here. The bright sun shines down, 
blanketing you with its life-giving warmth. Running parallel to the Southern Mountains, the highway 
meanders through the lower boundaries of the basin of civilization. The ground is smoothed by time, 
by feet, by beasts of burden, all of whom continually press down upon any vegetation who dares to 
try to shoot a sprout up in the path of commerce. A small path leads to the hamlet of Stewartsville,
a cosy little farming village amongst the flat fields of the southern plains. From here, the sound 
of children laughing can be heard. Attached to a wooden post here is a large metal bell. A young 
female horse with a snow white tail stands here, pawing the ground. A blackthorn sapling clings 
tenaciously to the ground here. Krellan Ysav'rai, Talons of Crow is here, shrouded. He wields an 
athame dagger in his left hand and a mystic cudgel in his right. Pruxi, Echo of the Wyrd is here, 
shrouded. He wields an elegant jet black viola in his left hand and a wyrden teacup in his right. 
Ruiku towers here. He wields a twisted staff in his left hand and a wyrm emblazoned shield in his 
right.
You see exits leading north, east, and west.

In the trees above path to Stewartsville.
The shadowy outline of a twisted forest casts a dark gloom here. The bright sun shines down, 
blanketing you with its life-giving warmth. A dusty path leads away from the highway in a well-paved
fashion that lends credence to the belief that it was handmade. Several white stones line the 
pathway in perpendicular lines that are carefully measured with carved signs that point toward a 
destination further along its flowing route. The encroaching flora and fauna normally so prevalent 
on these avenues have been carefully harvested and cut back to form a respectful delineation between
road and scrub. Pruxi, Echo of the Wyrd is here, shrouded. He wields an elegant jet black viola in 
his left hand and a wyrden teacup in his right. He is surrounded by one reflection of himself. 
Krellan Ysav'rai, Talons of Crow is here, shrouded. He wields an athame dagger in his left hand and 
a mystic cudgel in his right.

5896h, 5213m, 6240e, 10p, 26140en, 27279w exkb-
Before the Master Ravenwood Tree. (lost) (Glomdoring Forest.)
The bright sun shines down, blanketing you with its life-giving warmth. The dark heart of Glomdoring
Forest is almost audibly beating in this, its shadowy centre. Tall, blackened trees surround this 
clearing, pressing together into an imposing barrier of rotten vegetation. Moulds and fungi are 
smeared across the plants, their pungent stench suffusing the forest. The branches are coated in 
dark slime, slick tendrils that hang downwards. Although a variety of trees might actually grow 
here, the black tar that coats them renders them indistinguishable. A thin black mist creeps between
the trees, hanging low across the ground. The floor of the clearing itself is simply bare earth, 
cracked and dry. Overshadowing all is the Master Ravenwood Tree itself, jutting into the sky like a 
twisted fist. The sound of laughing crows echoes down from the treetops, a harsh sound for the ears 
below. The atmosphere vibrates with a palpable power. Brennan Stormcrow paces here, his cadaverous 
body twitching with sudden jerks. The Master Ravenwood Tree towers over everything here, pulsing 
with an immeasurable yet dark power. There are 12 dark nighthags here. A mature rowan tree stands 
proudly here. Casting darkness all around, a shadow totem thrusts up from the ground, chilling the 
air. There are 3 black direwolves here. His sinister red eyes constantly moving about the area, a 
shadowlord pauses here. A giant bat hangs here, wings folded about its body and one beady eye open. 
There are 2 illithoid scourges here. Nekai at the ready, an illithoid shade stands guard here. 
Covered in bone armour, a green eyelash viper is slithering about here. An ancient and skeletal tree
surrounded by bushes of glittering black roses stands tall against the test of time. There are 8 
shadowlord widowriders here. In the shape of an open palm, a metallic sigil lies here. Mushrooms are
growing here in a perfect circle. An animated skeleton stands here with a ghostly outline of a bat 
around its skull. An animated skeleton stands here with a ghostly outline of a beetle around its 
skull. An animated skeleton stands here with a ghostly outline of a spider around its skull. An 
animated skeleton stands here with a ghostly outline of a wasp around its skull. Surrounded by 
domothean death energies, an enormous map of the Catacombs of the Dead stretches across the open 
air. Sidd towers here. He wields a klangaxe of darkened steel with both hands.
You see a single exit leading north.

Path to farm. (Village of Stewartsville.)
The shadowy outline of a twisted forest casts a dark gloom here. The bright sun shines down, 
blanketing you with its life-giving warmth. Further along the path the twists reveal the farmhouse 
in the distance. Gleaming tile lines the roof in a sparkling pattern befitting a profitable home. 
Wired fences follow the pathway in a mirrored image and several animals lift their heads nosing the 
wind to catch the new scents. Piles of hay lie stacked about the lands in large bundles to provide 
food to those who might need it. The beautiful song of birds graces the pathway with a virtual 
concerto of musical delight. A blackthorn sapling clings tenaciously to the ground here. A graceful 
tree stands here, shaped vaguely like the form of a woman. A jet black spider with a deadly stinger 
scuttles about here, clicking his mandibles together. Talan Ysav'rai is here, shrouded. She wields 
an athame dagger in her left hand. Spirit Warden Xenthos An'Ryshe, the Ebon Strategist is here. He 
wields a baleful rapier of darkened steel in each hand. Urazial Inseira is here, shrouded. He wields
a glittering blackthorn lyre in his left hand and a wyrden shield of the seasons in his right. Nyir

crow wings in her left hand and a mystic cudgel in her right. Krellan Ysav'rai, Talons of Crow is

Path to farm. (Village of Stewartsville.)
There is a maelstrom of rainbow colours whipping violently around. The shadowy outline of a twisted 
forest casts a dark gloom here. The bright sun shines down, blanketing you with its life-giving 
warmth. A muddy path lined with cart tracks leads towards the farm in the distance. The obvious 
original source for the various food goods that are so prevalent within town, its rustic appearance 
hides an underlying truly modern and efficient production line. Several cows wander about in bovine 
fashion, large bells dangling with a strangely melodic ring that echoes throughout the area. Huge 
areas marked for planting lie in both directions and are breath-taking when viewed as a whole. A 
rowan sapling clings tenaciously to the ground here. A graceful tree stands here, shaped vaguely 
like the form of a woman. Swathed in the unholy black fires of Nil, a fallen pegasus regards the 
area with grim intensity. A demure willowisp floats lazily in the air here, bound by shadows. 
Massive black skeletal wings filling much of the space around her, a savage hippogriff stands here, 
her tail swishing idly. Spirit Warden Xenthos An'Ryshe, the Ebon Strategist is here. He wields a 
baleful rapier of darkened steel in each hand. Pruxi, Echo of the Wyrd is here, shrouded. He wields 
an elegant jet black viola in his left hand and a wyrden teacup in his right. Nyir Ysav'rai, Keeper 
of the Black Nest towers here, shrouded. She wields a dark shield in the form of crow wings in her 
left hand and a mystic cudgel in her right. Overseer Kalaneya Nightshade is here, shrouded. She 
wields a bloodlotus nekai in each hand. Talan Ysav'rai is here. She wields an athame dagger in her 
left hand. Priestess Nori Stormcrow, Initiate of Night's Secrets is here. Lady Nienla Nightshade, 
the Shadow of Silence is here, shrouded. Krellan Ysav'rai, Talons of Crow is here, shrouded. He 
wields an athame dagger in his left hand and a mystic cudgel in his right.
You see exits leading east and west.

5896h, 5943m, 6240e, 10p, 25521en, 26191w exkb-
Path to farm. (Village of Stewartsville.)
The shadows have been gathered here. There is a maelstrom of rainbow colours whipping violently arou
nd. The shadowy outline of a twisted forest casts a dark gloom here. The bright sun shines down, 
blanketing you with its life-giving warmth. A muddy path lined with cart tracks leads towards the 
farm in the distance. The obvious original source for the various food goods that are so prevalent 
within town, its rustic appearance hides an underlying truly modern and efficient production line. 
Several cows wander about in bovine fashion, large bells dangling with a strangely melodic ring that
echoes throughout the area. Huge areas marked for planting lie in both directions and are 
breath-taking when viewed as a whole. A rowan sapling clings tenaciously to the ground here. A 
graceful tree stands here, shaped vaguely like the form of a woman. A demure willowisp floats lazily
in the air here, bound by shadows. Massive black skeletal wings filling much of the space around 
her, a savage hippogriff stands here, her tail swishing idly. A young female horse with a snow white
tail stands here, pawing the ground. Spirit Warden Xenthos An'Ryshe, the Ebon Strategist is here. He
wields a baleful rapier of darkened steel in each hand. Pruxi, Echo of the Wyrd is here, shrouded. 
He wields an elegant jet black viola in his left hand and a wyrden teacup in his right. Overseer 
Kalaneya Nightshade is here, shrouded. She wields a bloodlotus nekai in each hand. Lady Nienla 
Nightshade, the Shadow of Silence is here, shrouded. Priestess Nori Stormcrow, Initiate of Night's 
Secrets is here. Talan Ysav'rai is here. She wields an athame dagger in her left hand. Krellan 
Ysav'rai, Talons of Crow is here, shrouded. He wields an athame dagger in his left hand and a mystic
cudgel in his right. Nyir Ysav'rai, Keeper of the Black Nest towers here, shrouded. She wields a 
dark shield in the form of crow wings in her left hand and a mystic cudgel in her right.
You see exits leading east and west.

5896h, 5843m, 5512e, 9p, 25384en, 25899w exkb-
Path to farm. (Village of Stewartsville.?)
The shadowy outline of a twisted forest casts a dark gloom here. A smattering of clouds fills the 
sky, lacing it with spiderwebs of grey. Further along the path the twists reveal the farmhouse in 
the distance. Gleaming tile lines the roof in a sparkling pattern befitting a profitable home. Wired
fences follow the pathway in a mirrored image and several animals lift their heads nosing the wind 
to catch the new scents. Piles of hay lie stacked about the lands in large bundles to provide food 
to those who might need it. The beautiful song of birds graces the pathway with a virtual concerto 
of musical delight. A blackthorn sapling clings tenaciously to the ground here. A graceful tree 
stands here, shaped vaguely like the form of a woman. A jet black spider with a deadly stinger 
scuttles about here, clicking his mandibles together. A demure willowisp floats lazily in the air 
here, bound by shadows. Wyrden Snare Toracu d'Syr, Ward of the Wyrd is here, shrouded. He wields a 
flying dragon klangaxe with both hands. Urazial Inseira is here, shrouded. He wields a glittering 
blackthorn lyre in his left hand and a wyrden shield of the seasons in his right. Spirit Warden 
Xenthos An'Ryshe, the Ebon Strategist is here. He wields a baleful rapier of darkened steel in each 
hand. Priestess Nori Stormcrow, Initiate of Night's Secrets is here. She wields an athame dagger in 
her left hand. Pruxi, Echo of the Wyrd is here, shrouded. He wields an elegant jet black viola in 
his left hand and a wyrden teacup in his right. Krellan Ysav'rai, Talons of Crow is here, shrouded. 
He wields an athame dagger in his left hand and a mystic cudgel in his right. Overseer Kalaneya 
Nightshade is here, shrouded. She wields a bloodlotus nekai in each hand. Talan Ysav'rai is here, 
shrouded. She wields an athame dagger in her left hand. Nyir Ysav'rai, Keeper of the Black Nest 
towers here, shrouded. She wields a dark shield in the form of crow wings in her left hand and a 
mystic cudgel in her right.

There is a maelstrom of rainbow colours whipping violently around. This location is flooded with 
deep, crystal blue water. The bright sun shines down, blanketing you with its life-giving warmth. A 
gnarled crimson spider with a glistening stinger scuttles about here, dripping venom from her 
mandibles. A demure willowisp floats lazily in the air here, bound by shadows. A skeletal, white 
stallion with leathery wings stands firm here. A jet black spider with a deadly stinger scuttles 
about here, clicking his mandibles together. The soul of Urazial roams the land, bodiless. Pruxi, 
Echo of the Wyrd is here, shrouded. He wields an elegant jet black viola in his left hand and a 
wyrden teacup in his right. Scordatura Pizzicato, Narsrim D'cente`, Crescendo of Transformation 
towers here, shrouded. He wields a darkwood mandolin encased in iron filigree and bone in his left 
hand and a Wand of Illusions in his right. Ruiku towers here. He wields a twisted staff in his left 
hand and a wyrm emblazoned shield in his right. Lord Fist Romero, Dark Prince of Demons is here. He 
wields a damning symbol of domination in his left hand. Father Talkan La'Saet towers here, shrouded.
He wields an ivory symbol bearing a black and gold trimmed amphora in his left hand. Krellan 
Ysav'rai, Talons of Crow is here, shrouded. He wields an athame dagger in his left hand and a mystic
cudgel in his right. General Vathael Valtyros, Knife of Fain is here, shrouded. He wields a hideous 
hammer of depraved steel in each hand.
